***круглый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:круглый.html>кру́глый</a> (1183)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*krǫglъ</i>; synchronically analysable as <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:круг.html>круг</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">krug</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-лый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-lyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">крѫглъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">krǫglŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">кру́глий</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">krúhlyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bulgarian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Bulgarian language">Bulgarian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="bg">кръ́гъл</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="bg-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">krǎ́gǎl</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Serbo-Croatian" class="extiw" title="w:Serbo-Croatian">Serbo-Croatian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="sh">окру́гао</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Slovene_language" class="extiw" title="w:Slovene language">Slovene</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sl">krógǝl</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Czech_language" class="extiw" title="w:Czech language">Czech</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cs">okrouhlý</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">krągły</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:круглый.html>кру́глый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">krúglyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)кругле́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)кругле́й</b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:самый.html>са́мый</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:круглый.html>кру́глый</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>round</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> perfect, complete</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:круговерть.html>кругове́рть</a> (31432)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:круг.html>круг</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">krug</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">circle</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-верт</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-vert</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, based on a combining form of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вертеть.html>верте́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vertétʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to turn</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:круговерть.html>кругове́рть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">krugovértʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:круговерть.html>кругове́рти</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:круговерть.html>кругове́рти</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:круговерть.html>кругове́ртей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dialectal<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> circular movement, whirlwind, gyre</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> cycle, whirlwind</li></ol>

***круговой.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:круговой.html>кругово́й</a> (12729)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:круг.html>круг</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">krug</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ово́й</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:круговой.html>кругово́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">krugovój</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>circular
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:круговой.html>кругово́е</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:движение.html>движе́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>krugovóje</b> dvižénije</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>circular</b> motion</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:круговой.html>кругова́я</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:оборона.html>оборо́на</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>krugovája</b> oboróna</i> ― <span class="e-translation">all-round defence</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally"><b>circular</b> defence</span>”)</div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:круговой.html>кругово́й</a></b> ча́ртер</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>krugovój</b> čártɛr</i> ― <span class="e-translation">round trip charter</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally"><b>circular</b> charter</span>”)</div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:круговой.html>кругова́я</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:панорама.html>панора́ма</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>krugovája</b> panoráma</i> ― <span class="e-translation">cyclorama, <b>circular</b> panorama</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:круговой.html>кругова́я</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:диаграмма.html>диагра́мма</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>krugovája</b> diagrámma</i> ― <span class="e-translation">pie chart</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally"><b>circular</b> diagram</span>”)</div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:круговой.html>кругова́я</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:система.html>систе́ма</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:соревнование.html>соревнова́ний</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>krugovája</b> sistéma (sorevnovánij)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">round robin (competition)</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally"><b>circular</b> system (of competition)</span>”)</div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:кругозор.html>кругозо́р</a> (19688)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:круг.html>круг</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">krug</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">зор</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zor</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кругозор.html>кругозо́р</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">krugozór</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кругозор.html>кругозо́ра</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кругозор.html>кругозо́ры</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кругозор.html>кругозо́ров</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:горизонт.html>horizon</a>, look, purview, scope, sight
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:человек.html>челове́к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:широкий.html>широ́ким</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:кругозор.html>кругозо́ром</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">čelovék s širókim <b>krugozórom</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">broad-minded person</span></div></dd>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b>кру́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>гом</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:наречие.html>Наре́чие</a>; неизменяемое.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-круг-</b>; суффикс: <b>-ом</b>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:кружево.html>кру́жево</a> (10347)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">круживо</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kruživo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv"><a href = vnd.unilang:круг.html>круг</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">krug</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">-иво</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кружево.html>кру́жево</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">krúževo</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кружево.html>кру́жева</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кружево.html>кружева́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кружево.html>кру́жев</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>lace
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">отде́лывать/<a href = vnd.unilang:отделать.html>отде́лать</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:платье.html>пла́тье</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:кружево.html>кружева́ми</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">otdélyvatʹ/otdélatʹ plátʹje <b>kruževámi</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to trim a dress <b>with lace</b></span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively<span class="ib-comma">,</span> poetic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> interlacing</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:кружение.html>круже́ние</a> (26828)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кружение.html>круже́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kružénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кружение.html>круже́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кружение.html>круже́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кружение.html>круже́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>going round, whirling, spinning</li></ol>

***кружить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:кружить.html>кружи́ть</a> (6473)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*krǫžiti</i> or <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:круг.html>круг</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">krug</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кружить.html>кружи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kružítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:закружить.html>закружи́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вскружить.html>вскружи́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to turn, to whirl, to spin, to wheel around
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:метель.html>мете́ль</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:кружить.html>кру́жит</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:кружить.html>кружи́т</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">metélʹ <b>krúžit/kružít</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">the snowstorm is whirling</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:кружить.html>кружи́ть</a></b> кому́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:голова.html>го́лову</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>kružítʹ</b> komú-libo gólovu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to turn someone's head</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to circle, to go round, to make circles</li>
<li>to wander</li></ol>

<div class="derivedterms" style="column-count: 2; -moz-column-count: 2; -ms-column-count: 2; -o-column-count: 2; -webkit-column-count: 2;;">

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b>кру<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:жить.html>жи́ть</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 4c.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́лы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:закружить.html>закружи́ть</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:окружить.html>окружи́ть</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>Также</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:использоваться.html>испо́льзуется</a> спряжение <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:схема.html>схе́ме</a> 4b:
</p>

<p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-круж-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:соорудить.html>-и</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.
</p>

<p><b>кру<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:жить.html>жи́ть</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ся</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,  <a href = vnd.unilang:возвратный.html>возвра́тный</a>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 4c.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующего</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́ла</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нет.html>нет</a>.

</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-круж-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:соорудить.html>-и</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b>; постфикс: <b>-ся</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<p><b>кру́ж<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ный</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:прилагательное.html>Прилага́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. </p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-круж-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:порядочный.html>-н</a></b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ый</b>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:крупа.html>крупа</a> (10571)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*krupa</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*krowpeh₂</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крупа.html>крупа́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">krupá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крупа.html>крупы́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крупа.html>кру́пы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крупа.html>круп</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>cereals, grits, groats</li>
<li>sleet</li></ol>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">крупча́тка</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">krupčátka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">крупорушка</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">kruporuška</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крупинка.html>крупи́нка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">krupínka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крупинка.html>крупи́нки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крупинка.html>крупи́нки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крупинка.html>крупи́нок</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>grain
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ни.html>ни</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:крупинка.html>крупи́нки</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:правда.html>пра́вды</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ni krupínki právdy</i> ― <span class="e-translation">not a grain of truth</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крупица.html>крупи́ца</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">krupíca</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крупица.html>крупи́цы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крупица.html>крупи́цы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крупица.html>крупи́ц</a></b>)

<li>a grain <i>(of)</i>, a little

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:крупнейший.html>крупне́йший</a> (4116)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крупнейший.html>крупне́йший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">krupnéjšij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">superlative degree of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крупный.html>кру́пный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">krúpnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:крупа.html>круп</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>не́й</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ший</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:прилагательное.html>Прилага́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:относительный.html>относи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. </p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:крупный.html>кру́пный</a> (649)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*krupьnъ</i>, equivalent to <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крупа.html>круп</a>(<a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>а</a>)</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">krup(a)</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крупный.html>кру́пный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">krúpnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)крупне́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)крупне́й</b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крупнейший.html>крупне́йший</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>coarse, coarse-grained</li>
<li>big, massive; numerous; large-scale</li>
<li>important, prominent, great</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p><b>кру<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ти́ть</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 4c.       <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́лы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:скрутить.html>скрути́ть</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:закрутить.html>закрути́ть</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-крут-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:соорудить.html>-и</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

***крутить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:крутить.html>крути́ть</a> (4013)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крутить.html>крути́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">krutítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скрутить.html>скрути́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:закрутить.html>закрути́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to twist, to twirl, to roll up</li>
<li>to turn</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">imperfective only<span class="ib-comma">,</span> transitive or intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to whirl, to swirl</li>
<li>to go out, to have an affair</li>
<li>to trick</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вертеть.html>верте́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vertétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вращать.html>враща́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vraščátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<div class="derivedterms" style="column-count: 2; -moz-column-count: 2; -ms-column-count: 2; -o-column-count: 2; -webkit-column-count: 2;;">
<p><i>imperfective</i>

<p><b>кру<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ти́ть</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 4c.       <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́лы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:скрутить.html>скрути́ть</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:закрутить.html>закрути́ть</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-крут-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:соорудить.html>-и</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.
</p>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крутой.html>кру́то</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">krúto</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl form-of lang-ru comparative-form-of origin-кру́то" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)<a href = vnd.unilang:круча.html>кру́че</a></b>)

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> cool, smart, awesome</li></ol>

***крутой.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:крутой.html>круто́й</a> (1917)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*krǫtъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крутой.html>круто́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">krutój</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)<a href = vnd.unilang:круча.html>кру́че</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">круте́йший</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>steep</li>
<li>abrupt, sharp
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:крутой.html>круто́й</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:поворот.html>поворо́т</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>krutój</b> povorót</i> ― <span class="e-translation">sharp turn</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>drastic
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:крутой.html>круты́е</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мера.html>ме́ры</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>krutýje</b> méry</i> ― <span class="e-translation">drastic measures</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">of food</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> thick
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:крутой.html>круто́е</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:яйцо.html>яйцо́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>krutóje</b> jajcó</i> ― <span class="e-translation">hard-boiled egg</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:крутой.html>круто́е</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:тесто.html>те́сто</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>krutóje</b> tésto</i> ― <span class="e-translation">thick dough</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> tough; strong
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:крутой.html>круто́й</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ты</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:чувак.html>чува́к</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Krutój</b> ty čuvák!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">You’re a tough one!</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> important
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:теперь.html>тепе́рь</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:крутой.html>круто́й</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:со.html>со</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>мной</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:здороваться.html>здоро́вается</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On tepérʹ <b>krutój</b>, so mnoj ne zdoróvajetsja.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">He's a big shot now; he won't even say 'hi' to me.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> cool, excellent
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:крутой.html>круто́й</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>тебя́</a> прики́д, <a href = vnd.unilang:чувак.html>чува́к</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Krutój</b> u tebjá prikíd, čuvák!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Sick threads, man!</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:крутой.html>крута́я</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>тебя́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тачка.html>та́чка</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Krutája</b> u tebjá táčka!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">You've got an awesome car!</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">steep</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">стремни́стый</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">stremnístyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">abrupt</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:резкий.html>ре́зкий</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">rézkij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неожиданный.html>неожи́данный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">neožídannyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">drastic</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:суровый.html>суро́вый</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">suróvyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">(slang) excellent</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">клёвый</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">kljóvyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">нехилый</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">nexilyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

Зализняка — 1b/c'. <a href = vnd.unilang:сравнительный.html>Сравни́тельная</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:степень.html>сте́пень</a> — <i><a href = vnd.unilang:круча.html>кру́че</a>, покру́че</i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:круча.html>кру́ча</a> (16480)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крутой.html>круто́й</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">krutój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>-а</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-a</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крутой.html>круто́й</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">krutój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крутой.html>кру́то</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">krúto</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">кру́тость</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">krútostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b>кру́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ча</b>
